Dear All

You know that in TOC we would have four tests, each of 15 % weightage. 

As announced during the lecture class, your third test (i.e. Test-3) would be conducted on Friday, Oct 06, 2020, during the lecture hour (i.e. during 12 - 1 PM). The duration and mode of conduct of this test would be the same as that of Test-1 and Test-2. 

Needless to say, that the fourth Test would be conducted as per AUGSD schedule. 

The syllabus for Test-3 would be (primarily) CFG, deterministic PDA's, determinism and top-down parsing, determinism and bottom-up parsing.

Subject: 11481001315_CS F372: Marking scheme for test 1
From: "Janardan Prasad Misra . . (via Nalanda)" <noreply-nalanda1@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 16-11-2020, 18:21
To: "VARKEYCHAN JACOB ." <f20170828@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Reply-to: "Do not reply to this email"

11481001315_CS F372 » Forums » Announcements » Marking scheme for test 1
Picture of Janardan Prasad Misra . . 	
Marking scheme for test 1
by Janardan Prasad Misra . . - Monday, 16 November 2020, 5:50 PM
  	
PDF document solution for test1.pdf

For Q1:

Gant Chart   : if it is correct 3 marks have been given .

Wait time computation: if all computations are correct, 1 marks has been awarded provided gant chart is correct.

Normalized turnaround time : if all computations are correct, 1 marks has been awarded provided gant chart is correct.

 For Q2:  answers with completely correct reasoning have been given full marks. If answer is partly correct, partial marking has been done

For Q3.  Fare share scheduling; for the computation of starting priority, one marks has been given for the rest of the priority computation, 2 marks for each time interval has been given. If in any time interval, if one or more priority computation is wrong, one mark has been deducted.

Hi Everyone

I didn't uploaded the slides for a few of the lectures. The reason is that you might have noticed that many times I simply put a question on the slide, and then solve it using pen/tablet. In addition, my slides of the previous two lectures got corrupted  I don't know why).

11481001334_BITS F312 » Forums » Announcements » Exam Pattern for Compre
Picture of Bijoy Krishna Mukherjee 	
Exam Pattern for Compre
by Bijoy Krishna Mukherjee - Sunday, 6 December 2020, 8:50 PM
  	

Please note that the comprehensive exam will be taken in the following pattern in google form platform.

Part-1:  30 marks, first 30 minutes

(similar to T-1, T-2, T-3; 50% negative marks for incorrect answers)

Part-2:  35 marks, next 45 minutes 

(broad questions and numericals on ANN; to scan the answer scripts and upload in .pdf format)

Part-3:  25 marks, next 30 minutes

(broad questions and numericals on Optimization and Fuzzy Logic; to scan the answer scripts and upload in .pdf format)

Also note that you have to keep your camera on during the exam. Extra 5-6 minutes will be given to scan the answer scripts and upload for part-2 and part-3 each. It is the responsibility of the students to make sure that the scanned answer scripts are legible and not hazy.

Subject: 11481001316_CS F301: Assignment-1: Evaluation criteria, test case and marks list
From: "Vandana Agarwal . . (via Nalanda)" <noreply-nalanda1@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 08-12-2020, 19:33
To: "VARKEYCHAN JACOB ." <f20170828@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Reply-to: "Do not reply to this email"

11481001316_CS F301 » Forums » Announcements » Assignment-1: Evaluation criteria, test case and marks list
Picture of Vandana Agarwal . . 	
Assignment-1: Evaluation criteria, test case and marks list
by Vandana Agarwal . . - Tuesday, 8 December 2020, 6:58 PM
  	
Text file eval.txt

Evaluation criteria: The authenticated code submitted by the teams which was free from plagiarism was considered for evaluation. The credit has been given to the tested code as per the following criteria. Marks are awarded on the correctness of the results. The test case used in evaluation is attached herewith for your reference and self-assessment of your code. Inform me immediately, if you observe any discrepancy in the test case. The criteria and marks distribution are as follows

1. Grammar design and implementation(6M): The design of the appropriate grammar for the given language in terms of the production rules given by the teams in grammar.txt file, and its implementation in terms of designing the grammar ADT as array of linked list and readGrammar() function are  evaluated out of 6 marks. Most of the teams have attempted this successfully and have been awarded 6 marks.

2. Data structure design (4M): The data structure design is subjectively looked at especially the use of union data type in variant record structures of type expression and parse tree nodes comprising of data items of different types and widths. A total of 4 marks are given to data structure design.

3. Parse tree creation and printing (6M): The parse tree creation and traversal for the given input are tested using the output on the test case used for evaluation. This includes the tokeniseSourcecode() for reading and tokenizing the test case code.  The total marks for parse tree are 6. The traversal order mentioned by the teams in the coding details was considered for evaluation. However, marks were deducted appropriately if the required information was not visible in the output.

4. Type expression computation (7M): Type expressions for the different data types computed by tree traversal of the declaration statements for populating the type expression table are given credit, if they are visible in the output obtained by printing the table as per the required information format specified earlier. Any order of variables printed line by line has been considered irrespective of the implementation of type expression as hash table or lookup table. There are about 50 variables declared to be of different data types, of which some data types are semantically correct and some are incorrect. It is expected that the list contains all of these along with all necessary details. A total of 7 marks are given if all variables are listed along with their type expressions and other relevant details. Marks are appropriately deducted for missing or incorrect information.

5. Type error detection and reporting (7M): The tree traversal of assignment statements and accessing the type expression table for variable identifiers in the assignment statement for type error detection are given credit, if the output is clearly displaying the errors by line numbers and associated relevant details as per the specifications. This is given 7 marks. The line numbers comprising of type errors in the given test case are as follows

29/30/29-30 (any of these is considered correct for jagged array type definition error), similarly 34/36/34-38 and 42/46/42-46  for the other two types. Remaining errors are at line numbers 51, 55, 56, 57, 58, 61, 64, 66, 68, 70 and 72.


I have observed that a few codes have compatibility issues and many modules are suffering from segmentation faults. If you have obtained marks less than your expectations, please do not panic.  Most zeros are due to the segmentation faults your code displayed on my system in that module. The recheck requests should be uploaded through Nalanda at the new link open from tomorrow onwards for the next three days. 

Please feel free to write to me any issue you face regarding your marks. 

Recheck request: Genuine recheck request for assignment-1 code will be accepted  during December 9, 2020,  9:00 AM to December 12, 2020, 9:00 AM (Separate link provided on the main course page).

Marks list: Group wise marks are given below.

11481001316_CS F301 » Forums » Announcements » Pre-comprehensive marks total (CS F301)
Picture of Vandana Agarwal . . 	
Pre-comprehensive marks total (CS F301)
by Vandana Agarwal . . - Thursday, 17 December 2020, 10:50 AM
  	

All genuine recheck requests have been considered for reevaluation and necessary changes have been made in the marks. Few answer keys were modified earlier for regular quizzes considering the genuine reasons for the change. Scores obtained by the students in a few evaluation components were needed to be normalized as per the following details.

Class tests (1-8): All class test were conducted for maximum five marks each. The best six scores are added and normalized to three marks (1% weight) by multiplying the sum by a factor of 3/5.

Regular quizzes (1-6): Quizzes 1, 2, 4, 5 and 6 were conducted for maximum 18 marks each while the quiz 3 was conducted for 32 marks. Quiz 3 is therefore first normalized to 18 marks by multiplying by a factor of 18/32. The best 4 scores in quizzes are then added and normalized to 6 marks (2% weight) by multiplying the sum by a factor of 6/18 .

Special quiz: This special quiz was conducted for 15 marks towards a weight of 5%. Therefore this does not require any normalization.

Tests 1, 2 and 3: The tests 1 and 2 were conducted for maximum 30 marks each (10% weight for each test). Therefore, the tests 1 and 2 do not require any normalization. However, the test 3 was conducted for a maximum of 30 marks towards a weight of 15%. Therefore, test 3 marks are normalized to 45 marks.

Assignment-1: The assignment was conducted for a maximum of 30 marks (10% weight). Therefore, this does not require any normalization.

The course statistics is as follows

MAX 	173.2
Average 	126.3
Standard deviation 	24.1
MIN 	49.5


Please inform me if any discrepancy is observed in your marks. A link for reporting such issues will be made available on the Nalanda course page during 6:00 p.m. today to 6:00 p.m. tomorrow.

Comprehensive Examination (CS F301: Principles of Programming Languages)
by Vandana Agarwal . . - Friday, 18 December 2020, 7:52 AM
  	

Comprehensive examination will be conducted tomorrow as per the AUGSD guidelines. The details are as follows.

    Date: December 19, 2020 (FN)
    Day:  Saturday
    Time: 10:00 AM to 12:00 Noon
    Duration: 120 minutes
    Venue:  Google Meet link:  https://meet.google.com/zwh-kjxr-uip
    Mode: Open book
    Syllabus: All topics covered in Lectures 9 - 26  (Refer main course page for details)
    Weight: 36%
    Marks: 108 
    Platform for conducting the test: Google forms 
    Examination pattern: The examination will be conducted in parts which will include multiple choice, fill in the blanks, short and long answer type questions. Each subsequent part will be made available after a given interval, only after the submission of the previous part.

 Requirements: 

    Students are advised to ensure uninterrupted power supply and high speed network at their end to be able to write the test comfortably. 
    Students must follow the examination norms as per the institute guidelines. 
    Arrange your institute identity card, water bottle, calculator and pens etc. on your desk appropriately before the exam. 
    You may require a phone camera or a scanner to capture your handwritten answers as images/ pdf for submission for some questions. If you are asked to submit such answers, extra 10  minutes will be given to you for capturing the pictures of your solution and converting to pdf as well as uploading. 

Malpractice regulations: Malpractice regulations will apply as per the institute policy, if any student is found indulged in any such activity. 

Examination venue: Students are advised to join the above Google meet link. The link for the comprehensive examination will be available at 10:00 AM. Students are advised to join the above meeting link 10 minutes prior to the examination.

Instructions for Operating Systems Compree Exam

 

* Compree exam will be held on 21/12/20 from 10.00 AM to 12.00 noon

*The exam will consist of two parts

*Part A will be multiple choice questions and will be of 1 hour duration. It will consist of 50 MCQs. Each correct answer will carry +1 mark and each wrong answer will carry -1 mark. Not attempted questions will not carry any marks.

*At 9.50 AM the students should join Google meet at the following link:

https://meet.google.com/eyx-sucz-fka

*Part A will start at 10.00 AM. Students should login in their NEW nalanda account to take the test

*Part B will be long answers which have to be answered by hand and uploaded

*The time for attempting Part B and uploading the answers is 1 hour

*The Google form link for Part B will be shared through Google meet at 11.00AM

Subject: 11481001322_CS F415: Compre marks and guidelines
From: "Poonam Goyal . (via Nalanda)" <noreply-nalanda1@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 21-12-2020, 17:04
To: "VARKEYCHAN JACOB ." <f20170828@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Reply-to: "Do not reply to this email"

11481001322_CS F415 » Forums » Announcements » Compre marks and guidelines
Picture of Poonam Goyal . 	
Compre marks and guidelines
by Poonam Goyal . - Monday, 21 December 2020, 4:59 PM
  	


       I.          All rechecks for all the components are done. Check and report immediately.

      II.          All the copy cases in labs are given zero. No penalty is given as for now.

    III.          Copy cases for comprehensive exam are also given zero. No penalty is given as for now.

 

Marking for comprehensive exams.

1.      A measure and justification why this measure should be used. Answers which describe both clearly will fetch full marks.

2.      All four cases described in the question should be explained … how the proposed method would handle them. Answers which describe all four clearly will fetch full marks. Partial marks are given according to the appropriateness of the method.

3.      (a) No partial marking

(b) Marks given only if FP tree method is used to find frequent item sets. Partial marking has been done.

4.      Output of each algorithm has to be given with justification. Partially correct arguments are given partial marks.

5.      Ques 5

a.       50% marks for the answers which have only distance matrix

b.       Without justification and calculation only 2/6 marks are given

c.       Answers with proper justification and labeling as core, border and noise fetch full marks

d.       Ideal matrix – 3/5 marks, comparison with similarity matrix 2/5 marks

e.       Partial marks for partially correct confusion matrix

f.       Need to calculate 3rd NN for every point, plot them in sorted order and cut the graph. Without NN distance zero marks given.

 

If you wish to submit a recheck for comprehensive exam, first go through this document then only apply for it. Unnecessary recheck will lead to critical and final evaluation of the whole copy.

You can apply for recheck by tomorrow (22nd Dec 2020) 12 noon. Late requests will not be considered. (scores will be released by tonight)

See this post in context

From: "Janardan Prasad Misra . . (via Nalanda)" <noreply-nalanda1@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>

Reply-to: "Do not reply to this email"

11481001315_CS F372 » Forums » Announcements » compree solutions
Picture of Janardan Prasad Misra . . 	
compree solutions
by Janardan Prasad Misra . . - Monday, 28 December 2020, 5:56 PM
  	

Compree solutions are now uploaded on Nalanda. Marking scheme is as follows .

Q1.

Part A)                  1 marks each for correct base address, limit and DPL . For every other bits you lose 1/2  marks for each wrong representation

Part B :                 no partial marking

Part C :                  No partial marking . The correct answer is 3 and reason is given in solution sheet

Q2.

Part a:  no partial marking

Part B :                 if the no of bits in logical address  and its split up is wrong you get no marks. You must specify all the index multipliers PDBR bits properly. if anything is wrong you would lose 1 mark for each wrong value.

Part C , D, E and F : No partial marking

Q3.  No partial marking.

Q4. No partial marking

Guidelines for Quiz-I of Compiler Construction (CS F363)
by Shashank Gupta . - Friday, 19 February 2021, 5:33 PM
  	

The Quiz-I of CS F363 (Compiler Construction) is scheduled on February 22nd, 2021 (Monday) from 11:00 AM onwards. The quiz will be conducted through Google form and duration of Quiz is 30 minutes. Each student can join one of the following Google Meet link corresponding to their BITS ID at 10:50 AM. (10 minutes before the start of examination). Ensure Internet connectivity, camera, Laptop, and any other thing required. The test would be Open-Book and can contain short answer questions, long answer questions, MCQ’s, etc. Any announcement would be done using these links; so please have access to headphone during the test. The google form link can be only accessed from the chat box of Google meet sessions

From: Time Table <timetable@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 25-02-2021, 13:45
To: students@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in
CC: Associate Dean AUGSD <ad.augsd@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>, Associate Dean AGSRD Pilani <ad.agsrd@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>

Dear Students (2019 Batch & Earlier AND 2020 MBA Batch),
Please note that you must keep the Mercer Mettl proctoring tool remain on throughout the exam duration as mentioned by Instructor In-charge.  In case, IC has scheduled the exam in another platform (Google form, Nalanda, Canvas, etc.), you must not click on the submit button on the Mercer Mettl Platform until you complete the examination.  If anyone closes the window and obstructs proctoring, his/her test evaluation will be null & void and IC's decision will be final in this regard.


Associate Deans
AUGSD/AGSRD

DAA MID SEM EXAM INSTRUCTIONNS
by Abhishek Mishra . - Thursday, 4 March 2021, 9:35 PM
  	

Time: 90 minutes for the test + 15 minutes of extra time for scanning and uploading your solutions on Mettl. You should scan and upload your solution before proceeding to the next problem to keep your work saved in case of network failure. You can use your mobile phone or scanner only for scanning and uploading your solution.

	

OPEN BOOK INSTRUCTIONS: 

Hard Copy: You can use any printed or photocopied books, lecture notes, or handwritten notes.

Soft Copy: You can use any previously downloaded file (e-books, lecture notes, etc) for reading.

Machine: You can use only the machine on which you are giving the exam. Any other machine (laptop, desktop, tablet, mobile, calculator, etc.) is not allowed (except for scanning and uploading your solution on Mettl).

Internet Browsing: Not Allowed.


SYLLABUS:

All topics covered up to 27th Feb (The Maximum Flow Problem and the Ford-Fulkerson Algorithm).

You will shortly receive the START TEST link which will get activated sharp on March 6th, 2021 at 02:00 PM.  Make sure of your availability on your systems at 01:55 PM to avoid any delay.

In case, if someone is not getting that exam link, he/she should request for the same on my email. id

In addition, please refer the guidelines of Mid-Sem examination of Compiler Construction CS F363 as follows:

    Mode of Test: Closed Book (Internet Browsing, Hard/Soft Copies, etc. are strictly prohibited.)
    Time Duration: 02:00 PM - 03:40 PM (including scanning and uploading time)
    Syllabus: Course Content covered till Feb 26th, 2021.
    Maximum Weightage: 30%
    Maximum Marks: 60
    Upload Options: Only Single PDF to be uploaded on the Metll
    Total Question: 7
    Invigilation: Proctoring will be done on the Mercer Mettl and 360 degree view needs to be provided when requested by the invigilator.

Make sure that the test will automatically get stopped at 03:40 PM. 

GOOD LUCK!!!!!

Lab Exam Announcement
by Virendra S Shekhawat - Thursday, 8 April 2021, 4:38 PM
  	

Dear Students,

Lab Exam (Weightage: 15%) will be conducted in online mode as per the schedule on 11-04-2021 (SUNDAY) at 10:00 AM. The question paper will be available on the NALANDA-AWS portal and the solution to be uploaded there itself. This exam is coding-based, i.e., you have to write the code for the given problem statement as per the instructions provided in the question paper.

Thank you.

From: "Shashank Gupta . (via Nalanda)" <shashank.gupta@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 17-04-2021, 14:30
To: "VARKEYCHAN JACOB ." <f20170828@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Reply-to: "Shashank Gupta ."

11491001318_CS F363 » Forums » Announcements » Guidelines for Quiz II of Compiler Construction (CS F363)
Picture of Shashank Gupta . 	
Guidelines for Quiz II of Compiler Construction (CS F363)
by Shashank Gupta . - Saturday, 17 April 2021, 1:59 PM
  	

The Quiz-II of CS F363 (Compiler Construction) is scheduled on April 19th, 2021 (Monday) from 11:00 AM onwards.  Please read the following instructions:

- The test will be conducted through the Google Forms and duration of Quiz is 30 minutes. 

- Each student can join one of the following Google Meet link corresponding to their BITS ID at 10:45 AM. (15 minutes before the start of examination). 

Sr. No.
	

BITS ID (From -To)
	

Invigilator
	

Google Meet Link

1.
	

2015A7PS0120P- 2017B1A70991P
	

Dr. Shashank Gupta
	

https://meet.google.com/uaj-axne-hed

2.
	

2017B3A71005P- 2018A7PS0229P
	

Dr. Vinti Agarwal
	

testhttps://meet.google.com/tgt-qmxq-seq

3.
	

2018A7PS0230P- 2018A7PS1121P
	

Mr. Yemini Ashok
	

https://meet.google.com/whi-ifuu-fpj

- If anyone has difficulty in finding his/her BITS ID from any of the above three S.No., he/she can join any one of the above Google Meet Links.

- Attendance will be taken only in the first 15 minutes. The test will start sharply at 11:00 AM and will stop at 11:30 AM. No extra time will be given  (including those who are joining late in the meet). 

- Ensure Internet connectivity, camera, Laptop, and any other thing required. 

- The test would be Open-Book and can contain short answer questions, long answer questions, MCQ’s, etc. 

- Any announcement would be done using these links; so please have access to headphone during the test. 

- The google form link of attendance and Quiz II can be only accessed from the chat box of Google meet sessions.

Hi everyone, 

hope you are doing fine. I am getting a lot of emails regarding DAA Tutorial (1-3) Marks. Here are some clarifications regarding the same:

Tutorial 1: If your answer is different from the answers uploaded on Nalanda you got 6 marks and if you did skip any step, some marks are deducted, it can be 2 or 4  based on the number of steps you missed.

Tutorial 2: If you correctly wrote the time complexity and explanation of your approach, you received 16 marks otherwise 0.

Tutorial 3: Many students did not show all the steps of the tree making in part c and part b of question 2, in this case you only received 2 marks in part b and 2 marks in part c.

NOTE: If you only have any genuine query other than the things listed above then only mail me or Abhishek Sir otherwise we have to put some penalty. please match your answers carefully with the solution uploaded on Nalanda before sending any email.

Subject: 11491001318_CS F363: Course Content for Upcoming Comprehensive Exam of Compiler Construction
From: "Shashank Gupta . (via Nalanda)" <shashank.gupta@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 04-05-2021, 09:04
To: "VARKEYCHAN JACOB ." <f20170828@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Reply-to: "Shashank Gupta ."

11491001318_CS F363 » Forums » Announcements » Course Content for Upcoming Comprehensive Exam of Compiler Construction
Picture of Shashank Gupta . 	
Course Content for Upcoming Comprehensive Exam of Compiler Construction
by Shashank Gupta . - Tuesday, 4 May 2021, 8:34 AM
  	

Hi,

As per the recent announcement from AUGSD, we have decided to include the following course content for the upcoming comprehensive examination of Compiler Construction:

Bottom-up Parsers: LR(0), SLR(1), LALR(1) and CLR(1)

Syntax Directed Definitions (SDD) and Syntax Directed Translations (SDT)

Machine Independent Code Techniques, Basic Blocks, Liveness Analysis

Register Allocation, Instruction Selection, Garbage Collection

Please note that one should have enough knowledge about the other topics for the proper understanding of above mentioned topics.

The issue of final grading procedure for the students opting for Comprehensive examination is discussed with the HOD and any clarity related to this issue will be communicated to you soon.

DAA Mid Sem Question Order
by Abhishek Mishra . - Friday, 7 May 2021, 12:26 PM
  	

Dear Students,

Midsem Q2 (order of growth) and Q3 (insertion sort running time) appear in random order (Q2-Q3 or Q3-Q2) in your paper. Interpretation of marks in the xlsx sheet: Q2 and Q3 as they appear in your paper (it may or may not be in the same order as shown in the solution).

Midsem Q4 (Network Flow) and Q5 (Huffman Encoding) appear in random order (Q4-Q5 or Q5-Q4) in your paper. Interpretation of marks in the xlsx sheet: Q4 and Q5 as they appear in the solution (Q4: Network Flow and Q5: Huffman Encoding).

Abhishek

Guidelines for Regular Comprehensive Exam of Compiler Construction (CSF363)
by Shashank Gupta . - Saturday, 22 May 2021, 5:26 PM
  	

Dear Students of CS F363 (Who have applied for Regular Comprehensive ),

You will receive the START TEST link on Monday which will get activated sharp on May 25th, 2021 at 09:00 AM.  Make sure of your availability on your systems at 08:55 AM to avoid any delay.

In case, if someone is not getting that exam link, he/she should request for the same on my email. id

You need to write your answers on A4 size sheet paper and get it uploaded as single PDF on Google form.

In addition, please refer the guidelines of Regular Comprehensive examination of Compiler Construction CS F363 as follows:

    Mode of Test: Open Book: A candidate can only access-Soft copy slides and PDF the BITS library, mettl application. The student is NOT allowed to access any website or online content (including google, etc) Mobile phone is only allowed for scanning during the last 10 minutes.
    Time Duration: 09:00 AM - 11:10 AM (including scanning and uploading time)
    Syllabus: Refer the previous notice of course content dated May 4th, 2021
    Maximum Weightage: 40%
    Maximum Marks: 80
    Upload Options: Only Single PDF to be uploaded on the Google form 
    Invigilation: Proctoring will be done on the Mercer Mettl and 360 degree view needs to be provided when requested by the invigilator. If any candidate will be reported for online browsing during exam either by invigilator/Mettl report, NC will be awarded to that candidate.

Make sure that the test will automatically get stopped at 11:10 PM. The submissions will not be accepted through email in any case.

GOOD LUCK!!!!!

Subject: BITS Notice Board Announcement
From: Director Pilani <director@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 03-08-2021, 15:41
To: faculty@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in, staff@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in, Students at Pilani Campus <students@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>

Dear All,

We are happy to announce the launch of BITS notice board portal (https://onboard.bits-pilani.ac.in/). The portal will facilitate the posting of general notices to all the user community and to specific targeted groups.

Currently all the notices are sent through e-mail. The present system supports mainly three groups namely student, Faculty and staff. The mails can be sent to individual groups or to multiple groups. The present facility does not offer mail delivery to the fine grained targeted email groups causing the individual mailbox cluttering.  

The team of IPC and SDET has taken up a new initiative and they have created a portal which  aims to provide a single dashboard for the posting and access to the various notices/announcements.

To begin with , we intend to provide notice posting rights to Head of departments, division heads, faculty-in-charges  and unit heads. Once the facility is operationalized, the root email facility will be withdrawn. The individual faculty members will continue to use the Nalanda email/announcement  facility to send the course related communication to the students. 
Hoping for your kind cooperation.

With the best regards,

Sudhirkumar Barai
Director, BITS Pilani-Pilani Campus

Subject: IPC Notice
From: "Mail Admin @ Pilani Campus" <mailadmin@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
Date: 25-09-2021, 11:20
To: Students at Pilani Campus <students@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>, PhD Group Pilani Campus <phd@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>
CC: Yashvardhan Sharma <yash@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in>

Dear all,

 

At IPC, we strive hard to keep the IT Infrastructure and services up and running on round the clock basis . To know the  details of facilities available and services offered by the IPC team, please  visit the IPC  web site https://www.bits-pilani.ac.in/pilani/ipc/Home . Some of the important services offered are listed below 

 

  

1. iCMS is an inhouse developed  Complaint Management System. The system allows users to register Network related complaint at the iCMS  Portal  https://icms.bits-pilani.ac.in

The users can login to the portal using their Official BITS e-mail Id  to register the complaint. Once the complaint is registered , IPC technical staff  would attend the call and make an effort to resolve the issues. 

 

2. Computing Facilities Access : IPC Website at https://www.bits-pilani.ac.in/pilani/ipc/Home  provides the details of the  computing facility , services  and ICT Infrastructure across the Pilani campus . To get access to the computing facilities, it is requested to contact the IPC Operators at 01596-255292 (Email : ipcoptr@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in). 

 

3. BITS Notice boards:  BITS Notice Board portal has been deployed at (https://onboard.bits-pilani.ac.in/ ). All BITS Notices specific to students, faculty and staff will be displayed here.  The portal provides a mechanism for displaying department specific notices which can only be viewed by a person belonging to the department. Course Specific notices will still be available at LMS Portal (https://nalanda-aws.bits-pilani.ac.in/ ) 

 

4. Gmail Password policy:   As per the latest policy of the Institute all the users should create a password for their official GMail accounts, as per the following guidelines;

 

·         Passwords must not contain the user’s account name or parts of the user’s full name that exceed two consecutive characters
·         Be at least eight characters in length
·         Contain characters from at least three of the following four categories:
              o    English uppercase characters (A through Z)
              o    English lowercase characters (a through z)
              o    Base 10 digits (0 through 9)
              o    Non-alphabetic characters (for example, !, $, #, %)

 

Please contact the IPC Operator for any issue with your Gmail login/password at 01596-255292 (Email : ipcoptr@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in). 


5. IT Policy : 

 

This is to inform you all that use of unlicensed software is illegal  and IP right  violation of the owner . This has also been stated in the IT policy document  of the institute (https://www.bits-pilani.ac.in/Uploads/BITSUserITPolicy.pdf ).  The excerpts from the IT Policy document are given below.for your kind reference  . 

 

1.  Users are not allowed to install personal software for use on BITS Pilani’s computer systems. Users are not allowed to download / install unauthorized / pirated software for use on BITS Pilani’s computer systems and their personal system when it is connected with BITS Pilani’s network.

2.      Users shall not make unauthorized copies of copyrighted software and documents, except as permitted by law or by the owner of the copyright. Copyrighted materials belonging to the entities other than BITS Pilani may not, subject to the allowable exemptions, be transmitted by faculty, staff or students on BITS Pilani mail / internet system. Setting up a file sharing service (within LAN) which violates Intellectual property rights is not allowed. All users obtaining access to other companies’ or individuals’ materials must respect all copyrights and may not copy, retrieve, modify or forward copyrighted materials, except with permission of the copyright owner or as may be permitted under the appropriate law. Each user shall observe all terms and conditions of the license agreement, under which the license to use any copyrighted work has been obtained.

In case of any such violation ,the user shall solely be  held responsible and liable for the offence arising out of unlawful use of  copyrighted material / software. 


 For any urgent matters, please contact our IT Manager, Mr. Ravi Krishnamurthy at 01596-255317 ( Email : it.manager@pilani.bits-pilani.ac.in )

-- 
Dr. Yashvardhan Sharma
Faculty Incharge,
Information Processing Centre,
BITS-Pilani

Quiz 1
by Divyum Sharma . - Saturday, 2 October 2021, 6:35 PM
  	

Date: October 4 (during lecture hour)
Duration: 30 minutes
Nature: Open book
Syllabus: The syllabus comprises of material covered up to and including the lecture dated Sep 17. In terms of the handout, this covers Module 1 as well as Ch 9A,B,C and a portion of Ch 27A (definition of Mobius function, Propositions 4,5,6) from Module 2. 

Students who are not on-campus

    You are required to join Google Classroom and Mercer Mettl by 4.00 PM. Your videos must be switched on and 360 degree view must be presented whenever demanded by the invigilator. 
    The link from mettl  has already been sent - the assessment is `MATHF441_Quiz1’ although the sender is `Sem2_NUMBER_THEORY - BITS Pilani’. If you are off-campus and haven’t received the email, inform me before 11:00 am on October 3, 2021. 
    Off-campus students who do not join Mercer Mettl for the quiz will be deemed absent.
    Mutual communication, internet browsing is not allowed. You can use hard copy/e-copy of textbooks and lecture slides (hard-copy or from Google Classroom).
    The quiz duration is 30 minutes and you will be given extra 5 minutes to scan and upload your handwritten solutions. Do NOT look at the time left on Mercer Mettl as that is set differently.
    Be sure to write your name and ID number on each page of the submission; otherwise the submission won't be graded. You can keep pages ready with your name and ID number written on them.
    Multiple submissions will not be allowed; your first submission will be considered final.
    Do not leave Mercer Mettl until asked to do so.

Students who are on-campus

    All on-campus students are required to report to Room No. 6104 (NAB) before 4:00 PM. The performance of an on-campus student will be cancelled if they try to attempt the quiz online.
    Please follow COVID protocols.
    Bring your ID card. You can bring textbooks (hard copy of textbooks or printout of relevant chapters) and printouts of lecture slides.
    Quiz will be given 30 minutes from the start. No one will be allowed to leave until the quiz duration is over.

Picture of Divyum Sharma . 	
Notice for Mid-semester examination
by Divyum Sharma . - Monday, 18 October 2021, 12:01 PM
  	

Discrete Mathematical Systems (MATH F441)

Notice for Mid-semester examination

 1.     The mid-semester examination for this course will be conducted on Monday 25-10-2021 from 9.00 AM to 10.30 AM. The maximum possible marks are 30.

2.     The examination will be conducted in off-line mode (physically in classrooms on campus) only. The seating arrangement will be in accordance with AUGSD notice.

3.     The examination will be closed book. Please bring BITS ID cards. 

4.     The syllabus consists of Modules 1, 2, 3 and a portion of Module 4 (RSA and Hill Codes: Sections 10A and 8F of Textbook T1) of the handout. 

5.     If you are unable to return to campus to take the mid-semester exam, you have to apply for the make up examination on academic.bits-pilani.ac.in  by 24-10-2021.

6.     If you have returned to the campus but are unable to take the exam for genuine reasons, you have to apply by email with evidence for genuineness by 26-10-2021.
